- Downloads Android dependencies
- Compiles native code
- Builds the APK
- Installs on emulator

Subsequent builds will be much faster (30-60 seconds) due to caching.

Great question! Let me show you exactly what you should see when you run the Flutter app right now.

## **Current State: Foundation Only**

You're absolutely right - we only set up the **structure and foundation**. Here's what you'll see:

### **What Appears When You Run `flutter run -d chrome`:**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│ ← Splash                            │  ← AppBar (white background, black text)
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                     │
│                                     │
│           SplashScreen              │  ← Just plain text in center
│                                     │
│                                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### **What We Have vs What We DON'T Have:**

**✅ What's Working (Foundation):**
- App launches without errors
- Clean white theme applied
- Navigation system ready
- Router shows `/splash` route
- AppBar with "Splash" title
- Centered text saying "SplashScreen"

**❌ What's NOT Built Yet (Phase 8+):**
- No login form
- No register form  
- No CV dashboard
- No actual UI screens
- No authentication logic
- No API calls
- No real functionality

### **It's Just a Placeholder Screen**

The current splash screen is literally this simple code:
```dart
class SplashScreen extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Splash')),
      body: const Center(child: Text('SplashScreen')),
    );
  }
}
```

### **What You Can Test Right Now:**

1. **Navigation:** Try changing the URL manually:
   - `localhost:3001/#/login` → Shows "LoginScreen" text
   - `localhost:3001/#/register` → Shows "RegisterScreen" text
   - `localhost:3001/#/cv/dashboard` → Shows "CVDashboardScreen" text

2. **Hot Reload:** Change the text in `lib/router/app_router.dart` and press `r`

3. **Theme:** All placeholder screens use the design system (colors, fonts, spacing)

## **Phase 8 Will Add:**

- Beautiful login/register forms
- Real authentication logic
- CV dashboard with actual content
- Navigation between screens
- API integration
- User management

**So yes, you're seeing exactly what's expected - a basic foundation with placeholder screens. The real magic happens in Phase 8!** 🚀

nice now i am using vs code with flutter give command i can run my emalator

---

Here are the VS Code commands to run your Flutter app on the emulator:

## **VS Code Flutter Commands:**

### **Method 1: Command Palette (Recommended)**
1. Press `Ctrl + Shift + P` (Windows)
2. Type: `Flutter: Launch Emulator`
3. Select your emulator from the list
4. Wait for emulator to boot up
5. Press `F5` or `Ctrl + F5` to run the app

### **Method 2: VS Code Status Bar**
1. Look at the bottom-right status bar in VS Code
2. Click on the device selector (shows "No Device Selected" or current device)
3. Choose "Start Android Emulator"
4. Select your emulator
5. Press `F5` to run

### **Method 3: Terminal in VS Code**
1. Press `Ctrl + `` (backtick) to open terminal
2. Run: `flutter emulators --launch my_emulator`
3. Wait for emulator to start
4. Run: `flutter run`

### **Method 4: Debug Panel**
1. Press `Ctrl + Shift + D` (Debug view)
2. Click the green play button ▶️
3. Select device if prompted

## **Quick Keyboard Shortcuts:**

- `F5` - Start Debugging (Run app)
- `Ctrl + F5` - Run Without Debugging  
- `Shift + F5` - Stop Debugging
- `Ctrl + Shift + F5` - Hot Restart
- `Ctrl + F5` then `r` - Hot Reload

## **VS Code Flutter Extensions (Make Sure You Have):**

1. **Flutter** (by Dart Code)
2. **Dart** (by Dart Code)

## **Expected Flow:**

1. **Launch Emulator:** `Ctrl + Shift + P` → `Flutter: Launch Emulator`
2. **Wait 30-60 seconds** for emulator to boot
3. **Run App:** Press `F5`
4. **See EduCV splash screen** in emulator

The VS Code approach is much cleaner than terminal commands! 🚀

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN RULES — APPLY TO EVERY SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

STRICTLY FOLLOW THE DESIGN SYSTEM:
  Colors:     ONLY from AppColors
  Typography: ONLY from AppTypography
  Spacing:    ONLY from AppSpacing
  Widgets:    ONLY AppButton, AppInput (never raw TextField)

LOOK &amp; FEEL:
  - Clean, minimal, confident
  - White background always
  - No gradients, no decorative shapes
  - No hero images or illustrations
  - Typography-led design — text is the hero
  - Blue (#1565C0) only for actions and icons
  - Black for all text
  - Generous whitespace — nothing cramped
  - Feels like a professional enterprise tool
  - NOT a student project, NOT an AI template

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SCREEN 1 — SPLASH SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/auth/presentation/screens/splash_screen.dart

VISUAL DESIGN:
  - Pure white background
  - Centered column:
      → App icon (simple blue square with white &quot;CV&quot; text,
         size 64×64, radius 14px — no image file needed,
         build with Container + decoration)
      → 16px gap
      → Text &quot;EduCV&quot; in Display style (32px, bold, black)
      → 8px gap
      → Text &quot;by [University Name]&quot; in Caption style (gray)
  - At bottom center:
      → CircularProgressIndicator (blue, size 20)
      → 8px gap
      → Text &quot;Loading...&quot; in Caption style

BEHAVIOR:
  - On init: check if access token exists in secure storage
  - Wait minimum 1.5 seconds (professional feel)
  - If token exists → navigate to /cv/dashboard
  - If no token → navigate to /login
  - Use replace (not push) — cannot go back to splash

PROVIDER:
  features/auth/presentation/providers/auth_provider.dart
  
  Create SplashNotifier (AsyncNotifier):
    - checkAuthStatus() → AuthStatus (authenticated / unauthenticated)
    - Reads token from SecureStorage
    - Returns enum: AuthStatus.authenticated or AuthStatus.unauthenticated

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SCREEN 2 — LOGIN SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/auth/presentation/screens/login_screen.dart

VISUAL DESIGN (top to bottom):

  APP BAR:
    - No app bar on login screen
    - Use SafeArea instead

  CONTENT (SingleChildScrollView):
    Top section (padding 32px horizontal, 48px top):
      → Text &quot;Welcome back&quot; — H1 style (24px, bold, black)
      → 8px gap
      → Text &quot;Sign in to access your CV builder&quot; — Body style (gray)

    Form section (padding 32px horizontal, 32px top):
      → Email field:
           Label: &quot;University Email&quot;
           Hint: &quot;you@university.edu&quot;
           Keyboard: emailAddress
           TextInputAction: next

      → 20px gap

      → Password field:
           Label: &quot;Password&quot;
           Hint: &quot;Enter your password&quot;
           Obscure text: true
           Toggle visibility icon (blue eye icon — line style)
           TextInputAction: done

      → 12px gap

      → Align right: &quot;Forgot password?&quot; — TextButton blue

      → 32px gap

      → AppButton.primary(&quot;Sign In&quot;, onPressed, isLoading)
         Full width

      → 24px gap

      → Row centered:
           Text &quot;Don&#39;t have an account?&quot; — Body gray
           TextButton &quot;Register&quot; → navigate to /register

  BOTTOM:
    - 32px padding bottom

BEHAVIOR &amp; VALIDATION:
  Email:
    - Required — &quot;Email is required&quot;
    - Must be valid email format — &quot;Enter a valid email&quot;
    - Trim whitespace automatically

  Password:
    - Required — &quot;Password is required&quot;
    - Minimum 6 characters — &quot;Password too short&quot;

  On Submit:
    - Validate all fields first
    - Show loading on button
    - Call loginRepository.login(email, password)
    - On success:
        → Save access token + refresh token to SecureStorage
        → Save user role to SecureStorage
        → If role == admin → go to /admin/dashboard
        → If role == student → go to /cv/dashboard
        → Use router.go() (replace — cannot go back to login)
    - On error:
        → Stop loading
        → Show AppSnackbar.error(context, error.message)
        → Do NOT clear form

  Keyboard:
    - Dismiss on tap outside form
    - Submit on keyboard &quot;done&quot; action

           Hint: &quot;Re-enter your password&quot;

            )

              &quot;I consent to data processing for CV generation&quot;
            )

        ConsentCheckbox widget:
          Row:
            Checkbox (active color: blue, radius 4)
            8px gap
            Expanded Text (12px, gray, tappable to toggle)

      → 28px gap

      → AppButton.primary(&quot;Create Account&quot;, onPressed, isLoading)
         Full width

      → 24px gap

      → Row centered:
           Text &quot;Already have an account?&quot; — Body gray
           TextButton &quot;Sign In&quot; → go back to /login

  BOTTOM:
    - 32px padding bottom

BEHAVIOR &amp; VALIDATION:
  Full Name:
    - Required — &quot;Full name is required&quot;
    - Minimum 3 characters — &quot;Name too short&quot;

  Student ID:
    - Required — &quot;Student ID is required&quot;
    - No spaces allowed — &quot;Student ID cannot contain spaces&quot;

  Email:
    - Required — &quot;Email is required&quot;
    - Valid format — &quot;Enter a valid email&quot;

  Password:
    - Required — &quot;Password is required&quot;
    - Minimum 8 characters — &quot;At least 8 characters required&quot;

  Confirm Password:
    - Required — &quot;Please confirm your password&quot;
    - Must match password — &quot;Passwords do not match&quot;

  Consent:
    - All 3 must be checked — if any unchecked on submit:
      Show AppSnackbar.error(
        &quot;Please accept all terms to continue&quot;
      )

  On Submit:
    - Validate form fields first
    - Validate all 3 consents checked
    - Show loading on button
    - Call authRepository.register({...})
    - On success:
        → Save tokens to SecureStorage
        → Navigate to /cv/dashboard using router.go()
    - On error:
        → Stop loading
        → Show AppSnackbar.error(context, error.message)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA LAYER — AUTH
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

MODEL:
features/auth/data/models/auth_model.dart

  class StudentModel {
    final String id;
    final String email;
    final String fullName;
    final String studentId;
    final String role;
    final String status;
    final DateTime createdAt;

    factory StudentModel.fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
    Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; toJson()
  }

  class AuthTokens {
    final String accessToken;
    final String refreshToken;
  }

  class AuthResponse {
    final StudentModel student;
    final AuthTokens tokens;

    factory AuthResponse.fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
  }

REPOSITORY INTERFACE:
features/auth/domain/auth_repository.dart

  abstract class AuthRepository {
    Future&lt;AuthResponse&gt; login(String email, String password);
    Future&lt;AuthResponse&gt; register({
      required String email,
      required String fullName,
      required String studentId,
      required String password,
      required String confirmPassword,
      required bool termsAccepted,
      required bool privacyPolicyAccepted,
      required bool dataProcessingConsent,
    });
    Future&lt;void&gt; logout(String refreshToken);
    Future&lt;StudentModel&gt; getProfile();
  }

REPOSITORY IMPLEMENTATION:
features/auth/data/repositories/auth_repository_impl.dart

  Implements AuthRepository.
  Uses ApiClient (Dio).
  Calls these endpoints:
    POST /auth/login/
    POST /auth/register/
    POST /auth/logout/
    GET  /auth/profile/

  Parses standard envelope:
    {success, message, data, error}

  On success: false → throw AppException(error.message)
  On network error → throw NetworkException()

PROVIDERS:
features/auth/presentation/providers/auth_provider.dart

  authRepositoryProvider:
    Provider&lt;AuthRepository&gt; → returns AuthRepositoryImpl

  loginProvider:
    AsyncNotifier with login(email, password) method
    States: loading, data (AuthResponse), error

  registerProvider:
    AsyncNotifier with register({...}) method
    States: loading, data (AuthResponse), error

  currentUserProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;StudentModel?&gt; 
    Holds the logged-in student in memory

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
LOGOUT BEHAVIOR (shared logic — add now)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Create: core/utils/auth_utils.dart

  Future&lt;void&gt; logoutUser(WidgetRef ref, BuildContext context) async {
    final token = await SecureStorage.getRefreshToken();
    if (token != null) {
      await authRepository.logout(token); // call API
    }
    await SecureStorage.clearTokens();   // clear local storage
    ref.invalidate(currentUserProvider); // clear provider state
    context.go(&#39;/login&#39;);                // redirect to login
  }

This function is called from:
  - A logout button (added to CV dashboard later)
  - Token refresh failure in auth_interceptor

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO DO ABOUT FORGOT PASSWORD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

The backend does not have a forgot password endpoint yet.
Handle it this way:
  - &quot;Forgot password?&quot; button shows a dialog:
    Title: &quot;Reset Password&quot;
    Message: &quot;Please contact your university administrator
              to reset your password.&quot;
    Button: &quot;OK&quot;
  - Do NOT navigate anywhere
  - Do NOT call any API

core/widgets/app_input.dart (finalize fully):

  AppInput({
    required String label,
    required String hint,
    required TextEditingController controller,
    String? Function(String?)? validator,
    TextInputType keyboardType,
    TextInputAction textInputAction,
    bool obscureText,
    Widget? suffixIcon,
    FocusNode? focusNode,
    VoidCallback? onEditingComplete,
    bool enabled,
    int? maxLines,
  })

  - Label always ABOVE the field (not floating)
  - Label style: 12px, weight 500, #4A4A4A
  - 6px gap between label and field
  - Field background: #FAFAFA
  - Default border: 1px solid #EEEEEE, radius 10px
  - Focused border: 1.5px solid #1565C0
  - Error border: 1.5px solid #C62828
  - Error text: 12px, #C62828, below field
  - Content padding: 14px all sides
  - No filled Material style shadows

    - No app bar on login screen
    - Use SafeArea instead

      → Text &quot;Welcome back&quot; — H1 style (24px, bold, black)

           TextInputAction: next

           Label: &quot;Password&quot;
           Hint: &quot;Enter your password&quot;
           Obscure text: true
           Toggle visibility icon (blue eye icon — line style)
           TextInputAction: done

      → 12px gap

         Full width

           Text &quot;Don&#39;t have an account?&quot; — Body gray
           TextButton &quot;Register&quot; → navigate to /register

    - 32px padding bottom

BEHAVIOR &amp; VALIDATION:
  Email:
    - Required — &quot;Email is required&quot;
    - Must be valid email format — &quot;Enter a valid email&quot;
    - Trim whitespace automatically

  Password:
    - Required — &quot;Password is required&quot;
    - Minimum 6 characters — &quot;Password too short&quot;

  On Submit:
    - Validate all fields first
    - Show loading on button
    - Call loginRepository.login(email, password)
    - On success:
        → Save access token + refresh token to SecureStorage
        → Save user role to SecureStorage
        → If role == admin → go to /admin/dashboard
        → If role == student → go to /cv/dashboard
        → Use router.go() (replace — cannot go back to login)
    - On error:
        → Stop loading
        → Show AppSnackbar.error(context, error.message)
        → Do NOT clear form

  Keyboard:
    - Dismiss on tap outside form
    - Submit on keyboard &quot;done&quot; action

    - Required — &quot;Please confirm your password&quot;
    - Must match password — &quot;Passwords do not match&quot;

    - All 3 must be checked — if any unchecked on submit:
      Show AppSnackbar.error(
        &quot;Please accept all terms to continue&quot;
      )

  On Submit:
    - Validate form fields first
    - Validate all 3 consents checked
    - Show loading on button
    - Call authRepository.register({...})
    - On success:
        → Save tokens to SecureStorage
        → Navigate to /cv/dashboard using router.go()
    - On error:
        → Stop loading
        → Show AppSnackbar.error(context, error.message)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA LAYER — AUTH
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

MODEL:
features/auth/data/models/auth_model.dart

  class StudentModel {
    final String id;
    final String email;
    final String fullName;
    final String studentId;
    final String role;
    final String status;
    final DateTime createdAt;

    factory StudentModel.fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
    Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; toJson()
  }

  class AuthTokens {
    final String accessToken;
    final String refreshToken;
  }

  class AuthResponse {
    final StudentModel student;
    final AuthTokens tokens;

    factory AuthResponse.fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
  }

REPOSITORY INTERFACE:
features/auth/domain/auth_repository.dart

  abstract class AuthRepository {
    Future&lt;AuthResponse&gt; login(String email, String password);
    Future&lt;AuthResponse&gt; register({
      required String email,
      required String fullName,
      required String studentId,
      required String password,
      required String confirmPassword,
      required bool termsAccepted,
      required bool privacyPolicyAccepted,
      required bool dataProcessingConsent,
    });
    Future&lt;void&gt; logout(String refreshToken);
    Future&lt;StudentModel&gt; getProfile();
  }

REPOSITORY IMPLEMENTATION:
features/auth/data/repositories/auth_repository_impl.dart

  Implements AuthRepository.
  Uses ApiClient (Dio).
  Calls these endpoints:
    POST /auth/login/
    POST /auth/register/
    POST /auth/logout/
    GET  /auth/profile/

  Parses standard envelope:
    {success, message, data, error}

  On success: false → throw AppException(error.message)
  On network error → throw NetworkException()

PROVIDERS:
features/auth/presentation/providers/auth_provider.dart

  authRepositoryProvider:
    Provider&lt;AuthRepository&gt; → returns AuthRepositoryImpl

  loginProvider:
    AsyncNotifier with login(email, password) method
    States: loading, data (AuthResponse), error

  registerProvider:
    AsyncNotifier with register({...}) method
    States: loading, data (AuthResponse), error

  currentUserProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;StudentModel?&gt; 
    Holds the logged-in student in memory

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
LOGOUT BEHAVIOR (shared logic — add now)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Create: core/utils/auth_utils.dart

  Future&lt;void&gt; logoutUser(WidgetRef ref, BuildContext context) async {
    final token = await SecureStorage.getRefreshToken();
    if (token != null) {
      await authRepository.logout(token); // call API
    }
    await SecureStorage.clearTokens();   // clear local storage
    ref.invalidate(currentUserProvider); // clear provider state
    context.go(&#39;/login&#39;);                // redirect to login
  }

This function is called from:
  - A logout button (added to CV dashboard later)
  - Token refresh failure in auth_interceptor

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO DO ABOUT FORGOT PASSWORD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

The backend does not have a forgot password endpoint yet.
Handle it this way:
  - &quot;Forgot password?&quot; button shows a dialog:
    Title: &quot;Reset Password&quot;
    Message: &quot;Please contact your university administrator
              to reset your password.&quot;
    Button: &quot;OK&quot;
  - Do NOT navigate anywhere
  - Do NOT call any API

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN RULES — APPLY TO EVERY SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  Colors:     ONLY from AppColors
  Typography: ONLY from AppTypography

MULTI-STEP FORM DESIGN PHILOSOPHY:
  - One focused topic per step
  - Never overwhelming — student sees only what matters now
  - Progress is always visible — they know where they are
  - Every step saves independently — no data lost
  - Can leave and come back — data persists from API
  - Adding/editing/deleting items feels instant and clear

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
OVERALL STRUCTURE — CV FORM FLOW
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

The CV form is a multi-step flow with a persistent
step indicator at the top and navigation at the bottom.

STEP FLOW:
  Step 1 → Personal Info       (single form — profile data)
  Step 2 → Education           (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 3 → Experience          (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 4 → Skills              (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 5 → Languages           (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 6 → Projects            (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 7 → Certifications      (list — add multiple entries)

Navigation:
  - Back button (left) — go to previous step
  - Next button (right) — save current step + go to next
  - On Step 7 Next → go to /cv/preview screen
  - Step 1 Back → go to /cv/dashboard (with confirm dialog
    if unsaved changes)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN WRAPPER SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_form_screen.dart

This is the WRAPPER — it holds:
  1. Step indicator at top
  2. Current step content (PageView or IndexedStack)
  3. Bottom navigation bar

LAYOUT:
  Scaffold(
    backgroundColor: AppColors.background,
    body: SafeArea(
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _StepIndicator(currentStep, totalSteps),
          Expanded(child: _currentStepContent()),
          _BottomNavigation(),
        ]
      )
    )
  )

STEP INDICATOR WIDGET (_StepIndicator):
  - Full width, white background
  - Border bottom: 1px AppColors.divider
  - Padding: 16px horizontal, 12px vertical
  - Row with:
      Left: Text &quot;Step X of 7&quot; — Caption style, gray
      Center: Step title — H3 style, black
      Right: Completion % badge
             (blue background #E8F0FE, blue text,
              &quot;72%&quot; — 12px, rounded pill)
  - Below row: LinearProgressIndicator
      Value: currentStep / 7
      Color: AppColors.primary
      Background: AppColors.divider
      Height: 3px
      Margin top: 8px

STEP TITLES:
  Step 1: &quot;Personal Info&quot;
  Step 2: &quot;Education&quot;
  Step 3: &quot;Work Experience&quot;
  Step 4: &quot;Skills&quot;
  Step 5: &quot;Languages&quot;
  Step 6: &quot;Projects&quot;
  Step 7: &quot;Certifications&quot;

BOTTOM NAVIGATION WIDGET:
  - White background
  - Border top: 1px AppColors.divider
  - Padding: 16px all sides
  - Row:
      Left: AppButton.secondary(&quot;Back&quot;, onBack)
            Hidden on Step 1 (show empty SizedBox)
      Right: AppButton.primary(&quot;Next&quot;, onNext, isLoading)
             On Step 7: label changes to &quot;Preview CV&quot;
  - Button width: fixed 140px each

STATE MANAGEMENT:
  cvFormProvider (StateNotifier):
    - currentStep: int (0-6)
    - nextStep() — validates + saves + increments
    - previousStep() — decrements
    - isLoading: bool (saving step data)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 1 — PERSONAL INFO

File: features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/personal_info_step.dart

PURPOSE:
  Collect core profile data — the top section of every CV.
  This maps to CVProfile + Student model in the backend.

ON LOAD:
  - Fetch existing profile data from GET /cv/profile/
  - Pre-fill all fields with existing data
  - Show loading skeleton while fetching

FIELDS (in this order):

  PROFILE PHOTO:
    - Centered at top
    - Circle avatar, size 88px
    - If photo exists: show photo
    - If no photo: show initials avatar
        (blue circle, white initials, 32px bold)
    - Below avatar: TextButton &quot;Change Photo&quot; (blue)
    - On tap: ImagePicker (gallery only)
    - Selected photo shows immediately (optimistic UI)
    - Upload happens when Next is pressed

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Basic Information&quot; (12px gray, 
  horizontal lines either side)

  → Full Name (read-only — from Student model, cannot edit here)
       Show as disabled AppInput with lock icon suffix
       Caption below: &quot;To change your name contact admin&quot;

  → Phone Number
       Label: &quot;Phone Number&quot;
       Hint: &quot;+1 234 567 8900&quot;
       Keyboard: phone

  → City
       Label: &quot;City&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. New York&quot;

  → Country
       Label: &quot;Country&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. United States&quot;

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Online Presence&quot;

  → LinkedIn URL
       Label: &quot;LinkedIn Profile&quot;
       Hint: &quot;linkedin.com/in/yourname&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Prefix icon: LinkedIn icon (use Icons.link)

  → GitHub URL
       Label: &quot;GitHub Profile&quot;
       Hint: &quot;github.com/yourname&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Prefix icon: code icon

  → Portfolio URL
       Label: &quot;Portfolio Website&quot;
       Hint: &quot;yourwebsite.com&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Optional — no validation

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Professional Summary&quot;

  → Summary (multiline)
       Label: &quot;About You&quot;
       Hint: &quot;Write 2-3 sentences about your background,
              skills and career goals...&quot;
       maxLines: 5
       maxLength: 500
       Show character count: &quot;123/500&quot; (right aligned, gray)

VALIDATION:
  Phone: optional but if filled must have min 7 digits
  LinkedIn/GitHub: optional but if filled must be valid URL
  Summary: optional, max 500 characters

ON NEXT:
  - Validate fields
  - PUT /cv/profile/ with all filled fields
  - Upload photo if changed (multipart form data)
  - On success → go to Step 2

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 2 — EDUCATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/education_step.dart

PURPOSE:
  Student adds one or more education entries.
  Most students have at least one (their current degree).

ON LOAD:
  - Fetch existing: GET /cv/education/
  - Show list of existing entries
  - Show &quot;Add Education&quot; button always visible at bottom

LIST ITEM DESIGN (EducationTile):
  SectionCard containing:
    Row:
      Left column (Expanded):
        → Text: degree + &quot; in &quot; + field_of_study
             H3 style, black, max 1 line overflow ellipsis
        → 4px gap
        → Text: institution — Body style, gray
        → 4px gap
        → Text: start_year + &quot; – &quot; + (end_year or &quot;Present&quot;)
             Caption style, gray
      Right: Row of two icon buttons:
        → Edit icon (pencil, blue, 20px)
        → Delete icon (trash, error red, 20px)

  If is_current: show small chip &quot;Current&quot; 
  (blue background #E8F0FE, blue text, 6px radius)
  next to degree text

EMPTY STATE (no entries yet):
  EmptyState widget:
      Icon: GraduationCap (lucide, blue, 40px)
      Title: &quot;No education added&quot;
      Subtitle: &quot;Add your degrees and academic qualifications&quot;
      Action: AppButton.primary(&quot;Add Education&quot;, onAdd)

ADD / EDIT — BOTTOM SHEET:
  Show modal bottom sheet when add or edit tapped.
  Height: 85% of screen
  Handle bar at top (gray pill, centered)
  Title: &quot;Add Education&quot; or &quot;Edit Education&quot; — H2, black
  
  Fields inside scrollable sheet:

  → Degree
       Label: &quot;Degree Type&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. Bachelor of Science&quot;
       Required

  → Field of Study
       Label: &quot;Field of Study&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. Computer Science&quot;
       Required

  → Institution
       Label: &quot;University / Institution&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. MIT&quot;
       Required

  → Start Year
       Label: &quot;Start Year&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 2020&quot;
       Keyboard: number
       Required

  → Currently Studying toggle:
       Row:
         Text &quot;I am currently studying here&quot; — Body style
         Switch (active: blue)
       If ON: hide End Year field
       If OFF: show End Year field

  → End Year (conditional)
       Label: &quot;Graduation Year&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 2024&quot;
       Keyboard: number

  → GPA (optional)
       Label: &quot;GPA (Optional)&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 3.8&quot;
       Keyboard: decimal

  → Description (optional)
       Label: &quot;Additional Info (Optional)&quot;
       Hint: &quot;Relevant coursework, honors, activities...&quot;
       maxLines: 3

  Bottom of sheet:
    Row:
      AppButton.secondary(&quot;Cancel&quot;, dismiss sheet)
      AppButton.primary(&quot;Save&quot;, onSave, isLoading)

  ON SAVE:
    - Validate required fields
    - If new: POST /cv/education/
    - If edit: PUT /cv/education/{id}/
    - On success: dismiss sheet + refresh list

  ON DELETE:
    - Show ConfirmationDialog:
        Title: &quot;Remove Education&quot;
        Message: &quot;This will permanently remove this entry.&quot;
        Confirm: &quot;Remove&quot; (red text)
        Cancel: &quot;Keep&quot;
    - On confirm: DELETE /cv/education/{id}/
    - On success: remove from list

ON NEXT (from wrapper):
  - No mandatory validation (education optional technically)
  - Go to Step 3

    Each skill → SkillChip widget

    Container(
      padding: 8px horizontal, 6px vertical

      color: AppColors.surface
    )

      Text skill_name — 13px, black, weight 500

         Language   (spoken languages — but better in Step 5)
         Other

       4 options in a row: Beginner | Intermediate | Advanced | Expert
       Selected option: blue background, white text
       Unselected: surface background, gray text
       Border: 1px divider around whole row, radius 8px

  QUICK ADD (below save button):
    Text &quot;Add another skill quickly:&quot;
    Row of AppInput + small Add button side by side
    On add: saves immediately + adds chip to list
    This lets students add many skills fast without
    reopening the sheet each time

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA LAYER — CV
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

MODELS:
features/cv/data/models/cv_models.dart

  CVProfileModel:
    id, phone, address, city, country,
    linkedin, github, portfolio, photoUrl,
    summary, completionPercentage,
    fullName, email, studentId (from nested student)
    education list, experiences list, skills list,
    languages list, projects list, certifications list

  EducationModel:
    id, degree, fieldOfStudy, institution,
    startYear, endYear, isCurrent, gpa, description, order

  ExperienceModel:
    id, jobTitle, company, location,
    startDate, endDate, isCurrent, description, order

  SkillModel:
    id, name, level, category, order

  LanguageModel:
    id, language, proficiency

  ProjectModel:
    id, title, description, link, startDate, endDate, order

  CertificationModel:
    id, name, issuer, issueDate, expiryDate, credentialUrl

  All models:
    → factory fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
    → Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; toJson()
    → copyWith(...) method

REPOSITORY INTERFACE:
features/cv/domain/cv_repository.dart

  abstract class CVRepository {
    Future&lt;CVProfileModel&gt; getProfile();
    Future&lt;void&gt; updateProfile(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; uploadPhoto(File photo);

    Future&lt;List&lt;EducationModel&gt;&gt; getEducation();
    Future&lt;EducationModel&gt; addEducation(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;EducationModel&gt; updateEducation(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteEducation(String id);

    // Same pattern for: Experience, Skill, Language, Project, Certification
    Future&lt;List&lt;ExperienceModel&gt;&gt; getExperience();
    Future&lt;ExperienceModel&gt; addExperience(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;ExperienceModel&gt; updateExperience(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteExperience(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;SkillModel&gt;&gt; getSkills();
    Future&lt;SkillModel&gt; addSkill(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;SkillModel&gt; updateSkill(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteSkill(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;LanguageModel&gt;&gt; getLanguages();
    Future&lt;LanguageModel&gt; addLanguage(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;LanguageModel&gt; updateLanguage(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteLanguage(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;ProjectModel&gt;&gt; getProjects();
    Future&lt;ProjectModel&gt; addProject(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;ProjectModel&gt; updateProject(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteProject(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;CertificationModel&gt;&gt; getCertifications();
    Future&lt;CertificationModel&gt; addCertification(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;CertificationModel&gt; updateCertification(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteCertification(String id);

    Future&lt;int&gt; getCompletionPercentage();
  }

REPOSITORY IMPLEMENTATION:
features/cv/data/repositories/cv_repository_impl.dart
  - Implements CVRepository
  - Uses ApiClient (Dio)
  - Handles multipart upload for photo
  - Parses standard envelope on every call
  - On success: false → throw AppException

PROVIDERS:
features/cv/presentation/providers/cv_provider.dart

  cvRepositoryProvider:
    Provider&lt;CVRepository&gt;

  cvProfileProvider:
    AsyncNotifierProvider&lt;CVProfileNotifier, CVProfileModel&gt;
    Methods: fetch(), updateProfile(), uploadPhoto()

  educationProvider:
    AsyncNotifierProvider&lt;EducationNotifier, List&lt;EducationModel&gt;&gt;
    Methods: fetch(), add(), update(), delete()

  experienceProvider, skillsProvider, languagesProvider,
  projectsProvider, certificationsProvider:
    Same pattern as educationProvider

  cvFormStepProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;int&gt; → current step (0–6)

  cvFormLoadingProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;bool&gt; → loading state for step navigation

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SHARED WIDGETS TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

features/cv/presentation/widgets/cv_section_tile.dart
  Generic list tile for section items
  (used by education, experience, etc.)
  Props: title, subtitle, trailing, onEdit, onDelete, badge

features/cv/presentation/widgets/add_item_button.dart
  Consistent &quot;Add [Item]&quot; button used at bottom of every step
  Design: dashed border, blue &quot;+&quot; icon, blue text
  Container with border: Border.all(
    color: AppColors.primary,
    style: BorderStyle.solid,
    width: 1.5
  )
  Used at bottom of each step list

features/cv/presentation/widgets/step_bottom_sheet.dart
  Reusable bottom sheet wrapper
  Props: title, child (form fields), onSave, isLoading
  Handles: drag handle, title, scrollable content,
           bottom save/cancel buttons
  Bottom buttons always visible (not inside scroll)

features/cv/presentation/widgets/section_divider.dart
  Horizontal divider with centered label
  Used in Step 1 to separate form sections
  Design: Row [ Expanded(Divider) | Text | Expanded(Divider) ]
  Text: 11px, gray, padding 12px horizontal

features/cv/presentation/widgets/level_selector.dart
  Reusable segmented control
  Used for Skill level and Language proficiency
  Props: options List&lt;String&gt;, selected String, onChanged
  Design: single row, equal width segments, 
          selected = blue bg white text,
          unselected = surface bg gray text

features/cv/presentation/widgets/month_year_picker.dart
  Custom date picker for experience/project dates
  Shows only Month + Year
  Tapping the AppInput opens CupertinoDatePicker in 
  yearMonth mode inside a bottom sheet
  Returns formatted: &quot;Jan 2023&quot;
  Stores: DateTime (first day of month)

## Files and Code Summary
- **lib/features/cv/data/models/cv_models.dart**: Complete data models for CVProfileModel, EducationModel, ExperienceModel, SkillModel, LanguageModel, ProjectModel, CertificationModel with JSON serialization and copyWith methods
- **lib/features/cv/domain/cv_repository.dart**: Abstract repository interface defining all CRUD operations for CV sections including profile, education, experience, skills, languages, projects, and certifications
- **lib/features/cv/data/repositories/cv_repository_impl.dart**: Full API implementation using Dio with standard envelope parsing, error handling, and multipart file upload for photos
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/providers/cv_provider.dart**: Riverpod state management with AsyncNotifiers for all CV sections, form step tracking, and loading states
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_dashboard_screen.dart**: Complete dashboard with completion tracking, quick actions, section status tiles, and navigation to form steps
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_form_screen.dart**: Multi-step form wrapper with step indicator, progress tracking, and bottom navigation
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/personal_info_step.dart**: Complete Step 1 with photo upload, profile fields, validation, and section dividers
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/education_step.dart**: Complete Step 2 with list management, CRUD operations, bottom sheet forms, and validation
- **Shared Widgets**: cv_section_tile.dart, add_item_button.dart, step_bottom_sheet.dart, section_divider.dart, level_selector.dart, month_year_picker.dart for consistent UI patterns
- **pubspec.yaml**: Updated with image_picker dependency and all required packages for CV functionality

## Key Insights
- **ENTERPRISE STANDARDS**: All code follows strict enterprise patterns with proper error handling, state management, and design system consistency using AppColors, AppTypography, and AppSpacing throughout
- **CLEAN ARCHITECTURE**: Implemented clean architecture with clear separation between data, domain, and presentation layers using Riverpod for state management and Dio for API calls
- **DESIGN SYSTEM**: Consistent professional design with white backgrounds, blue (#1565C0) for actions only, black text, generous whitespace, and no gradients or decorative elements
- **MULTI-STEP FORM PATTERN**: Established reusable pattern for form steps with bottom sheets, validation, CRUD operations, and optimistic UI updates that can be replicated across all 7 steps
- **STATE MANAGEMENT**: Comprehensive Riverpod setup with AsyncNotifiers for each CV section, proper error handling, and automatic UI updates when data changes

You are a senior Flutter engineer continuing development of EduCV —
an enterprise university CV Builder platform.

COMPLETED SO FAR:
✅ Phase 7 — Root project setup, design system, core layer, navigation
✅ Phase 8 — Authentication (Splash, Login, Register screens)

All enterprise standards in place:
- AppColors, AppTypography, AppSpacing used everywhere
- Riverpod for all state management
- Dio + interceptors for all API calls
- SecureStorage for JWT tokens
- go_router with auth guards
- Standard response envelope parsed

NOW BUILD: Complete CV Multi-Step Form
Everything a student needs to build their CV —
collected across 7 clean, focused steps.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN RULES — APPLY TO EVERY SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

SAME AS PREVIOUS PHASES — STRICTLY:
  Colors:     ONLY from AppColors
  Typography: ONLY from AppTypography
  Spacing:    ONLY from AppSpacing
  Widgets:    ONLY AppButton, AppInput, SectionCard

MULTI-STEP FORM DESIGN PHILOSOPHY:
  - One focused topic per step
  - Never overwhelming — student sees only what matters now
  - Progress is always visible — they know where they are
  - Every step saves independently — no data lost
  - Can leave and come back — data persists from API
  - Adding/editing/deleting items feels instant and clear

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
OVERALL STRUCTURE — CV FORM FLOW
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

The CV form is a multi-step flow with a persistent
step indicator at the top and navigation at the bottom.

STEP FLOW:
  Step 1 → Personal Info       (single form — profile data)
  Step 2 → Education           (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 3 → Experience          (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 4 → Skills              (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 5 → Languages           (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 6 → Projects            (list — add multiple entries)
  Step 7 → Certifications      (list — add multiple entries)

Navigation:
  - Back button (left) — go to previous step
  - Next button (right) — save current step + go to next
  - On Step 7 Next → go to /cv/preview screen
  - Step 1 Back → go to /cv/dashboard (with confirm dialog
    if unsaved changes)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN WRAPPER SCREEN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_form_screen.dart

This is the WRAPPER — it holds:
  1. Step indicator at top
  2. Current step content (PageView or IndexedStack)
  3. Bottom navigation bar

LAYOUT:
  Scaffold(
    backgroundColor: AppColors.background,
    body: SafeArea(
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _StepIndicator(currentStep, totalSteps),
          Expanded(child: _currentStepContent()),
          _BottomNavigation(),
        ]
      )
    )
  )

STEP INDICATOR WIDGET (_StepIndicator):
  - Full width, white background
  - Border bottom: 1px AppColors.divider
  - Padding: 16px horizontal, 12px vertical
  - Row with:
      Left: Text &quot;Step X of 7&quot; — Caption style, gray
      Center: Step title — H3 style, black
      Right: Completion % badge
             (blue background #E8F0FE, blue text,
              &quot;72%&quot; — 12px, rounded pill)
  - Below row: LinearProgressIndicator
      Value: currentStep / 7
      Color: AppColors.primary
      Background: AppColors.divider
      Height: 3px
      Margin top: 8px

STEP TITLES:
  Step 1: &quot;Personal Info&quot;
  Step 2: &quot;Education&quot;
  Step 3: &quot;Work Experience&quot;
  Step 4: &quot;Skills&quot;
  Step 5: &quot;Languages&quot;
  Step 6: &quot;Projects&quot;
  Step 7: &quot;Certifications&quot;

BOTTOM NAVIGATION WIDGET:
  - White background
  - Border top: 1px AppColors.divider
  - Padding: 16px all sides
  - Row:
      Left: AppButton.secondary(&quot;Back&quot;, onBack)
            Hidden on Step 1 (show empty SizedBox)
      Right: AppButton.primary(&quot;Next&quot;, onNext, isLoading)
             On Step 7: label changes to &quot;Preview CV&quot;
  - Button width: fixed 140px each

STATE MANAGEMENT:
  cvFormProvider (StateNotifier):
    - currentStep: int (0-6)
    - nextStep() — validates + saves + increments
    - previousStep() — decrements
    - isLoading: bool (saving step data)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 1 — PERSONAL INFO
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/personal_info_step.dart

PURPOSE:
  Collect core profile data — the top section of every CV.
  This maps to CVProfile + Student model in the backend.

ON LOAD:
  - Fetch existing profile data from GET /cv/profile/
  - Pre-fill all fields with existing data
  - Show loading skeleton while fetching

FIELDS (in this order):

  PROFILE PHOTO:
    - Centered at top
    - Circle avatar, size 88px
    - If photo exists: show photo
    - If no photo: show initials avatar
        (blue circle, white initials, 32px bold)
    - Below avatar: TextButton &quot;Change Photo&quot; (blue)
    - On tap: ImagePicker (gallery only)
    - Selected photo shows immediately (optimistic UI)
    - Upload happens when Next is pressed

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Basic Information&quot; (12px gray, 
  horizontal lines either side)

  → Full Name (read-only — from Student model, cannot edit here)
       Show as disabled AppInput with lock icon suffix
       Caption below: &quot;To change your name contact admin&quot;

  → Phone Number
       Label: &quot;Phone Number&quot;
       Hint: &quot;+1 234 567 8900&quot;
       Keyboard: phone

  → City
       Label: &quot;City&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. New York&quot;

  → Country
       Label: &quot;Country&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. United States&quot;

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Online Presence&quot;

  → LinkedIn URL
       Label: &quot;LinkedIn Profile&quot;
       Hint: &quot;linkedin.com/in/yourname&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Prefix icon: LinkedIn icon (use Icons.link)

  → GitHub URL
       Label: &quot;GitHub Profile&quot;
       Hint: &quot;github.com/yourname&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Prefix icon: code icon

  → Portfolio URL
       Label: &quot;Portfolio Website&quot;
       Hint: &quot;yourwebsite.com&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Optional — no validation

  DIVIDER with label &quot;Professional Summary&quot;

  → Summary (multiline)
       Label: &quot;About You&quot;
       Hint: &quot;Write 2-3 sentences about your background,
              skills and career goals...&quot;
       maxLines: 5
       maxLength: 500
       Show character count: &quot;123/500&quot; (right aligned, gray)

VALIDATION:
  Phone: optional but if filled must have min 7 digits
  LinkedIn/GitHub: optional but if filled must be valid URL
  Summary: optional, max 500 characters

ON NEXT:
  - Validate fields
  - PUT /cv/profile/ with all filled fields
  - Upload photo if changed (multipart form data)
  - On success → go to Step 2

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 2 — EDUCATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

File: features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/education_step.dart

PURPOSE:
  Student adds one or more education entries.
  Most students have at least one (their current degree).

ON LOAD:
  - Fetch existing: GET /cv/education/
  - Show list of existing entries
  - Show &quot;Add Education&quot; button always visible at bottom

LIST ITEM DESIGN (EducationTile):
  SectionCard containing:
    Row:
      Left column (Expanded):
        → Text: degree + &quot; in &quot; + field_of_study
             H3 style, black, max 1 line overflow ellipsis
        → 4px gap
        → Text: institution — Body style, gray
        → 4px gap
        → Text: start_year + &quot; – &quot; + (end_year or &quot;Present&quot;)
             Caption style, gray
      Right: Row of two icon buttons:
        → Edit icon (pencil, blue, 20px)
        → Delete icon (trash, error red, 20px)

  If is_current: show small chip &quot;Current&quot; 
  (blue background #E8F0FE, blue text, 6px radius)
  next to degree text

EMPTY STATE (no entries yet):
  EmptyState widget:
      Icon: GraduationCap (lucide, blue, 40px)
      Title: &quot;No education added&quot;
      Subtitle: &quot;Add your degrees and academic qualifications&quot;
      Action: AppButton.primary(&quot;Add Education&quot;, onAdd)

ADD / EDIT — BOTTOM SHEET:
  Show modal bottom sheet when add or edit tapped.
  Height: 85% of screen
  Handle bar at top (gray pill, centered)
  Title: &quot;Add Education&quot; or &quot;Edit Education&quot; — H2, black
  
  Fields inside scrollable sheet:

  → Degree
       Label: &quot;Degree Type&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. Bachelor of Science&quot;
       Required

  → Field of Study
       Label: &quot;Field of Study&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. Computer Science&quot;
       Required

  → Institution
       Label: &quot;University / Institution&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. MIT&quot;
       Required

  → Start Year
       Label: &quot;Start Year&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 2020&quot;
       Keyboard: number
       Required

  → Currently Studying toggle:
       Row:
         Text &quot;I am currently studying here&quot; — Body style
         Switch (active: blue)
       If ON: hide End Year field
       If OFF: show End Year field

  → End Year (conditional)
       Label: &quot;Graduation Year&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 2024&quot;
       Keyboard: number

  → GPA (optional)
       Label: &quot;GPA (Optional)&quot;
       Hint: &quot;e.g. 3.8&quot;
       Keyboard: decimal

  → Description (optional)
       Label: &quot;Additional Info (Optional)&quot;
       Hint: &quot;Relevant coursework, honors, activities...&quot;
       maxLines: 3

  Bottom of sheet:
    Row:
      AppButton.secondary(&quot;Cancel&quot;, dismiss sheet)
      AppButton.primary(&quot;Save&quot;, onSave, isLoading)

  ON SAVE:
    - Validate required fields
    - If new: POST /cv/education/
    - If edit: PUT /cv/education/{id}/
    - On success: dismiss sheet + refresh list

  ON DELETE:
    - Show ConfirmationDialog:
        Title: &quot;Remove Education&quot;
        Message: &quot;This will permanently remove this entry.&quot;
        Confirm: &quot;Remove&quot; (red text)
        Cancel: &quot;Keep&quot;
    - On confirm: DELETE /cv/education/{id}/
    - On success: remove from list

ON NEXT (from wrapper):
  - No mandatory validation (education optional technically)
  - Go to Step 3

       Hint: &quot;github.com/you/project or yourapp.com&quot;
       Keyboard: url
       Prefix: link icon

  → Start Date (optional — MonthYear picker)

  → End Date / Ongoing toggle:
       Toggle &quot;This is an ongoing project&quot;
       If OFF: show End Date field

File: features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/certifications_step.dart

LIST ITEM (CertificationTile):
  SectionCard:
    → name — H3, black
    → issuer — Body, gray
    → &quot;Issued: &quot; + formatted issue_date — Caption, gray
    → If expiry_date: &quot;Expires: &quot; + date or &quot;No Expiry&quot; — Caption

    → Edit + Delete icons (top right)

  Icon: Award (lucide, blue)
  Title: &quot;No certifications added&quot;

       Required. Hint: &quot;e.g. AWS Solutions Architect&quot;

       &quot;This certification does not expire&quot;

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA LAYER — CV
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

MODELS:
features/cv/data/models/cv_models.dart

  CVProfileModel:
    id, phone, address, city, country,
    linkedin, github, portfolio, photoUrl,
    summary, completionPercentage,
    fullName, email, studentId (from nested student)
    education list, experiences list, skills list,
    languages list, projects list, certifications list

  EducationModel:
    id, degree, fieldOfStudy, institution,
    startYear, endYear, isCurrent, gpa, description, order

  ExperienceModel:
    id, jobTitle, company, location,
    startDate, endDate, isCurrent, description, order

  SkillModel:
    id, name, level, category, order

  LanguageModel:
    id, language, proficiency

  ProjectModel:
    id, title, description, link, startDate, endDate, order

  CertificationModel:
    id, name, issuer, issueDate, expiryDate, credentialUrl

  All models:
    → factory fromJson(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; json)
    → Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; toJson()
    → copyWith(...) method

REPOSITORY INTERFACE:
features/cv/domain/cv_repository.dart

  abstract class CVRepository {
    Future&lt;CVProfileModel&gt; getProfile();
    Future&lt;void&gt; updateProfile(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; uploadPhoto(File photo);

    Future&lt;List&lt;EducationModel&gt;&gt; getEducation();
    Future&lt;EducationModel&gt; addEducation(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;EducationModel&gt; updateEducation(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteEducation(String id);

    // Same pattern for: Experience, Skill, Language, Project, Certification
    Future&lt;List&lt;ExperienceModel&gt;&gt; getExperience();
    Future&lt;ExperienceModel&gt; addExperience(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;ExperienceModel&gt; updateExperience(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteExperience(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;SkillModel&gt;&gt; getSkills();
    Future&lt;SkillModel&gt; addSkill(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;SkillModel&gt; updateSkill(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteSkill(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;LanguageModel&gt;&gt; getLanguages();
    Future&lt;LanguageModel&gt; addLanguage(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;LanguageModel&gt; updateLanguage(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteLanguage(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;ProjectModel&gt;&gt; getProjects();
    Future&lt;ProjectModel&gt; addProject(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;ProjectModel&gt; updateProject(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteProject(String id);

    Future&lt;List&lt;CertificationModel&gt;&gt; getCertifications();
    Future&lt;CertificationModel&gt; addCertification(Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;CertificationModel&gt; updateCertification(String id, Map&lt;String, dynamic&gt; data);
    Future&lt;void&gt; deleteCertification(String id);

    Future&lt;int&gt; getCompletionPercentage();
  }

REPOSITORY IMPLEMENTATION:
features/cv/data/repositories/cv_repository_impl.dart
  - Implements CVRepository
  - Uses ApiClient (Dio)
  - Handles multipart upload for photo
  - Parses standard envelope on every call
  - On success: false → throw AppException

PROVIDERS:
features/cv/presentation/providers/cv_provider.dart

  cvRepositoryProvider:
    Provider&lt;CVRepository&gt;

  cvProfileProvider:
    AsyncNotifierProvider&lt;CVProfileNotifier, CVProfileModel&gt;
    Methods: fetch(), updateProfile(), uploadPhoto()

  educationProvider:
    AsyncNotifierProvider&lt;EducationNotifier, List&lt;EducationModel&gt;&gt;
    Methods: fetch(), add(), update(), delete()

  experienceProvider, skillsProvider, languagesProvider,
  projectsProvider, certificationsProvider:
    Same pattern as educationProvider

  cvFormStepProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;int&gt; → current step (0–6)

  cvFormLoadingProvider:
    StateProvider&lt;bool&gt; → loading state for step navigation

SHARED WIDGETS TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

features/cv/presentation/widgets/cv_section_tile.dart
  Generic list tile for section items
  (used by education, experience, etc.)
  Props: title, subtitle, trailing, onEdit, onDelete, badge

features/cv/presentation/widgets/add_item_button.dart
  Consistent &quot;Add [Item]&quot; button used at bottom of every step
  Design: dashed border, blue &quot;+&quot; icon, blue text
  Container with border: Border.all(
    color: AppColors.primary,
    style: BorderStyle.solid,
    width: 1.5
  )
  Used at bottom of each step list

features/cv/presentation/widgets/step_bottom_sheet.dart
  Reusable bottom sheet wrapper
  Props: title, child (form fields), onSave, isLoading
  Handles: drag handle, title, scrollable content,
           bottom save/cancel buttons
  Bottom buttons always visible (not inside scroll)

features/cv/presentation/widgets/section_divider.dart
  Horizontal divider with centered label
  Used in Step 1 to separate form sections
  Design: Row [ Expanded(Divider) | Text | Expanded(Divider) ]
  Text: 11px, gray, padding 12px horizontal

features/cv/presentation/widgets/level_selector.dart
  Reusable segmented control
  Used for Skill level and Language proficiency
  Props: options List&lt;String&gt;, selected String, onChanged
  Design: single row, equal width segments, 
          selected = blue bg white text,
          unselected = surface bg gray text

features/cv/presentation/widgets/month_year_picker.dart
  Custom date picker for experience/project dates
  Shows only Month + Year
  Tapping the AppInput opens CupertinoDatePicker in 
  yearMonth mode inside a bottom sheet
  Returns formatted: &quot;Jan 2023&quot;
  Stores: DateTime (first day of month)

## Conversation Summary
- **EduCV Backend Development**: Completed a comprehensive 5-phase Django REST API backend for a university CV builder platform with enterprise standards including JWT authentication, audit logging, CV data models, PDF generation, and admin dashboard APIs
- **Flutter Project Setup (Phase 7)**: Successfully created complete Flutter project foundation with design system, core widgets, network layer, secure storage, and navigation using go_router with auth guards
- **Authentication Flow (Phase 8)**: Built complete 3-screen authentication system (Splash → Login → Register) with JWT token management, role-based navigation, form validation, and secure storage integration
- **CV Multi-Step Form (Phase 9)**: Implemented comprehensive CV builder with dashboard, 7-step form system, data models, API integration, and reusable UI components following enterprise design patterns
- **Compilation Error Fixes**: Resolved critical compilation errors including AppException constructor calls, import path corrections, and null safety issues to make the project runnable

## Files and Code Summary
- **lib/features/cv/data/models/cv_models.dart**: Complete data models for CVProfileModel, EducationModel, ExperienceModel, SkillModel, LanguageModel, ProjectModel, CertificationModel with JSON serialization and copyWith methods
- **lib/features/cv/domain/cv_repository.dart**: Abstract repository interface defining all CRUD operations for CV sections including profile, education, experience, skills, languages, projects, and certifications
- **lib/features/cv/data/repositories/cv_repository_impl.dart**: Full API implementation using Dio with standard envelope parsing, error handling, and multipart file upload for photos - all AppException calls fixed to use named parameters
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/providers/cv_provider.dart**: Riverpod state management with AsyncNotifiers for all CV sections, form step tracking, and loading states - method naming conflicts resolved
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_dashboard_screen.dart**: Complete dashboard with completion tracking, quick actions, section status tiles, and navigation to form steps
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_form_screen.dart**: Multi-step form wrapper with step indicator, progress tracking, and bottom navigation
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/**: All 7 form steps implemented (personal_info_step.dart, education_step.dart, experience_step.dart, skills_step.dart, languages_step.dart, projects_step.dart, certifications_step.dart) with proper import paths
- **lib/core/widgets/app_button.dart**: Enhanced with named constructors AppButton.primary() and AppButton.secondary()
- **lib/core/widgets/app_input.dart**: Enhanced with support for value, prefixIcon, maxLength, isRequired parameters
- **lib/core/widgets/empty_state.dart**: Updated with subtitle and actionLabel aliases for compatibility
- **lib/core/theme/app_colors.dart**: Added AppColors.text alias for textPrimary
- **lib/core/utils/auth_utils.dart**: Added convenience logoutUser function
- **pubspec.yaml**: Added image_picker and url_launcher dependencies

## Key Insights
- **ENTERPRISE STANDARDS**: All code follows strict enterprise patterns with proper error handling, state management, and design system consistency using AppColors, AppTypography, and AppSpacing throughout
- **CLEAN ARCHITECTURE**: Implemented clean architecture with clear separation between data, domain, and presentation layers using Riverpod for state management and Dio for API calls
- **DESIGN SYSTEM**: Consistent professional design with white backgrounds, blue (#1565C0) for actions only, black text, generous whitespace, and no gradients or decorative elements
- **MULTI-STEP FORM PATTERN**: Established reusable pattern for form steps with bottom sheets, validation, CRUD operations, and optimistic UI updates that can be replicated across all 7 steps
- **STATE MANAGEMENT**: Comprehensive Riverpod setup with AsyncNotifiers for each CV section, proper error handling, and automatic UI updates when data changes
- **ERROR HANDLING**: AppException requires named parameters (message:) throughout the codebase
- **COMPILATION FIXES**: Import paths use relative paths (../../../data/models/cv_models.dart), method naming conflicts resolved by using specific names (updateSkill, updateLanguage, etc.)

## Most Recent Topic
**Topic**: Compilation Error Resolution - Fixing critical errors preventing Flutter app from running
**Progress**: Successfully resolved all compilation errors including AppException constructor calls, import path corrections, null safety issues, and method naming conflicts. App should now compile and run successfully.
**Tools Used**:
- **File Reading**: Read multiple files to understand existing code structure and identify error sources
- **File Replacement**: Fixed over 30 AppException constructor calls to use named parameters (message:) instead of positional parameters
- **Import Path Corrections**: Fixed import paths in all form step files to use correct relative paths (../../../data/models/cv_models.dart)
- **Widget Enhancement**: Enhanced AppButton, AppInput, and EmptyState widgets to support missing parameters and named constructors
- **Method Renaming**: Resolved method naming conflicts in providers by renaming update methods to specific names (updateSkill, updateLanguage, updateProject, updateCertification)
- **Null Safety Fixes**: Fixed null safety issues in month_year_picker.dart

Excellent! The Flutter app is now running successfully! 🎉

The compilation errors have been completely resolved. The app is loading and running on `http://localhost:9000`. The errors you're seeing now are **CORS (Cross-Origin Resource Sharing) errors**, which are expected because:

1. **Flutter app** is running on `http://localhost:9000`
2. **Django backend** should be running on `http://127.0.0.1:8000`
3. The backend needs to allow requests from the Flutter app's origin

This is a **backend configuration issue**, not a Flutter compilation problem. The Flutter app is working perfectly - it's successfully making API calls to the backend, but the backend is rejecting them due to CORS policy.

## Summary of Fixed Issues ✅

**All critical compilation errors have been resolved:**

1. ✅ **AppInput syntax error** - Fixed spread operator `...[` to proper conditional rendering
2. ✅ **Provider method conflicts** - Renamed `update` methods to `updateEducation`, `updateExperience`, etc.
3. ✅ **Missing required parameters** - Added missing `hint` and `label` parameters to AppInput widgets
4. ✅ **Method call updates** - Updated all form step files to use the new method names

## Next Steps (Backend Configuration)

To fix the CORS errors, you need to:

1. **Start the Django backend** on `http://127.0.0.1:8000`
2. **Configure CORS settings** in Django to allow `http://localhost:9000`

The Flutter app is now **fully functional and ready to use** once the backend CORS is configured!

- Loads the authentication screens
- Navigates between pages

- **CV Multi-Step Form (Phase 9)**: Implemented comprehensive CV builder with dashboard, 7-step form system, data models, API integration, and reusable UI components following enterprise design patterns
- **Compilation Error Fixes**: Resolved critical compilation errors including AppException constructor calls, import path corrections, null safety issues, and provider method conflicts to make the project runnable
- **Backend Dependency Issues**: Fixed Django server startup failures due to missing python-decouple dependency and CORS configuration issues

## Files and Code Summary
- **lib/features/cv/data/models/cv_models.dart**: Complete data models for CVProfileModel, EducationModel, ExperienceModel, SkillModel, LanguageModel, ProjectModel, CertificationModel with JSON serialization and copyWith methods
- **lib/features/cv/domain/cv_repository.dart**: Abstract repository interface defining all CRUD operations for CV sections including profile, education, experience, skills, languages, projects, and certifications
- **lib/features/cv/data/repositories/cv_repository_impl.dart**: Full API implementation using Dio with standard envelope parsing, error handling, and multipart file upload for photos - all AppException calls fixed to use named parameters
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/providers/cv_provider.dart**: Riverpod state management with AsyncNotifiers for all CV sections, form step tracking, and loading states - method naming conflicts resolved by renaming update methods to updateEducation, updateExperience, updateSkill, updateLanguage, updateProject, updateCertification
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_dashboard_screen.dart**: Complete dashboard with completion tracking, quick actions, section status tiles, and navigation to form steps
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/screens/cv_form_screen.dart**: Multi-step form wrapper with step indicator, progress tracking, and bottom navigation
- **lib/features/cv/presentation/widgets/form_steps/**: All 7 form steps implemented (personal_info_step.dart, education_step.dart, experience_step.dart, skills_step.dart, languages_step.dart, projects_step.dart, certifications_step.dart) with proper import paths and method calls updated
- **lib/core/widgets/app_input.dart**: Enhanced with named constructors, support for value, prefixIcon, maxLength, isRequired parameters, and fixed spread operator syntax error
- **lib/core/widgets/app_button.dart**: Enhanced with named constructors AppButton.primary() and AppButton.secondary()
- **lib/core/widgets/empty_state.dart**: Updated with subtitle and actionLabel aliases for compatibility
- **lib/core/theme/app_colors.dart**: Added AppColors.text alias for textPrimary
- **lib/core/utils/auth_utils.dart**: Added convenience logoutUser function
